## 1. Executive Summary

### 1.1 Platform Overview

BidDeed.AI is an **Agentic AI ecosystem** for foreclosure auction intelligence, purpose-built for Everest Capital USA's Brevard County, Florida operations. The platform processes foreclosure auctions through a proprietary 12-stage methodology called **The Everest Ascentâ„¢**.

### 1.2 Business Value

| Metric | Value | Description |
|--------|-------|-------------|
| Extra Deals/Quarter | $50,000 | ML-identified opportunities |
| Avoided Losses/Quarter | $100,000 | Lien discovery protection |
| Time Savings | 40+ hrs/month | Automated analysis |
| Annual Platform Value | $300-400K | Combined benefits |
| System Operating Cost | $3,300/year | Infrastructure + APIs |
| **ROI** | **100x** | Value/Cost ratio |

### 1.3 Architecture Principles

1. **Agentic Design** - Autonomous AI agents with human-in-the-loop for critical decisions
2. **Event-Driven** - Loosely coupled services communicating via events
3. **Cost-Optimized** - Smart Router achieving 40-55% FREE LLM tier usage
4. **Fault-Tolerant** - Checkpointing and graceful degradation at every stage
5. **Secure-by-Design** - Layer 8 IP protection for business logic
6. **Observable** - Full telemetry across all system components

### 2.2 Architecture Tiers

| Tier | Purpose | Technologies | Deployment |
|------|---------|--------------|------------|
| **Presentation** | User interfaces | Next.js, React, Tailwind | Cloudflare Pages |
| **Orchestration** | Pipeline control | LangGraph, Python | GitHub Actions |
| **Services** | Data extraction | Python scrapers | GitHub Actions |
| **Data** | Persistence | Supabase, SQLite | Cloud hosted |
| **Infrastructure** | Execution env | GitHub Actions, CF | Cloud native |

---

### 5.3 Data Retention Policy

| Data Type | Retention Period | Storage Tier | Archival |
|-----------|------------------|--------------|----------|
| auction_results | 7 years | Hot | Cold after 1 year |
| historical_auctions | Indefinite | Hot | Used for ML training |
| pipeline_runs | 90 days | Hot | Archived to cold |
| insights | 1 year | Hot | Deleted |
| smart_router_logs | 30 days | Hot | Aggregated to metrics |
| daily_metrics | 3 years | Hot | Cold after 1 year |
| DOCX reports | 2 years | Cold | Deleted |

---

### 6.2 API Contracts

| Integration | Protocol | Format | Authentication | Rate Limit |
|-------------|----------|--------|----------------|------------|
| BECA Court | HTTPS | HTML/PDF | None | 10 req/min |
| BCPAO | REST | JSON | None | 60 req/min |
| AcclaimWeb | HTTPS | HTML | Session Cookie | 5 req/min |
| RealTDM | HTTPS | HTML | None | 30 req/min |
| Census API | REST | JSON | API Key | 50 req/day |
| Anthropic | REST | JSON | API Key | Per plan |
| Google AI | REST | JSON | API Key | 1500 req/day FREE |
| DeepSeek | REST | JSON | API Key | Per plan |
| Supabase | REST | JSON | Service Key | Unlimited |

## 9. Security Architecture


### 9.2 Secret Management

| Secret Type | Storage | Rotation | Access |
|-------------|---------|----------|--------|
| API Keys (LLM) | GitHub Secrets | 90 days | Workflow only |
| Supabase Keys | GitHub Secrets | 30 days | Workflow only |
| GitHub Token | Repository | On compromise | Workflow only |
| Cloudflare Keys | Cloudflare | 90 days | Dashboard only |
| Layer 8 Keys | Separate vault | Never (recreate) | Code only |

---

|-----------|--------|--------|--------|

### 11.2 Dashboard Metrics

| Dashboard | Metrics | Refresh |
|-----------|---------|---------|
| Pipeline Health | Success rate, duration, errors | Real-time |
| Cost Analytics | LLM spend by tier, daily/monthly | Hourly |
| Business KPIs | Recommendations, judgment value | Daily |
| ML Performance | Prediction accuracy, confidence | Weekly |

---

### 12.2 Environment Configuration

| Environment | Purpose | URL | Deployment |
|-------------|---------|-----|------------|
| Production | Live system | brevard-bidder-landing.pages.dev | Auto on main |
| Preview | PR review | [commit].pages.dev | Auto on PR |
| Development | Local testing | localhost:3000 | Manual |

## 13. API Specifications

### 13.1 REST API Endpoints

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: BidDeed.AI API
  version: 1.0.0
  description: Foreclosure Auction Intelligence API

servers:
  - url: https://brevard-bidder-landing.pages.dev/api
    description: Production

paths:
  /analyze:
    post:
      summary: Start pipeline analysis
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required:
                - case_number
                - address
              properties:
                case_number:
                  type: string
                  pattern: '^\d{2}-\d{4}-CA-\d{6}$'
                  example: "05-2024-CA-012345"
                address:
                  type: string
                  example: "123 Main St"
                city:
                  type: string
                  default: "Melbourne"
                zip_code:
                  type: string
                  pattern: '^\d{5}$'
                  default: "32940"
      responses:
        '202':
          description: Pipeline started
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                properties:
                  run_id:
                    type: string
                  status:
                    type: string
                    enum: [STARTED, QUEUED]
        '400':
          description: Invalid request
        '429':
          description: Rate limited

  /status/{run_id}:
    get:
      summary: Get pipeline status
      parameters:
        - name: run_id
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Pipeline status
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/PipelineStatus'
        '404':
          description: Run not found

  /auctions:
    get:
      summary: List auctions
      parameters:
        - name: date
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            format: date
        - name: status
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [UPCOMING, COMPLETED, ALL]
        - name: decision
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [BID, REVIEW, SKIP, ALL]
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Auction list
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: array
                items:
                  $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuctionSummary'

  /chat:
    post:
      summary: AI chat completion
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              required:
                - message
              properties:
                message:
                  type: string
                context:
                  type: object
                  properties:
                    case_number:
                      type: string
                    auction_date:
                      type: string
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Chat response
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: object
                properties:
                  response:
                    type: string
                  tier_used:
                    type: string
                  tokens_used:
                    type: integer

components:
  schemas:
    PipelineStatus:
      type: object
      properties:
        run_id:
          type: string
        case_number:
          type: string
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [RUNNING, COMPLETED, FAILED, CANCELLED]
        current_stage:
          type: integer
          minimum: 1
          maximum: 12
        progress_percent:
          type: integer
        stage_results:
          type: object
        recommendation:
          type: string
          enum: [BID, REVIEW, SKIP, DO_NOT_BID]
        max_bid:
          type: number
        confidence:
          type: number
        duration_seconds:
          type: integer
        error_message:
          type: string

    AuctionSummary:
      type: object
      properties:
        case_number:
          type: string
        auction_date:
          type: string
          format: date
        property_address:
          type: string
        final_judgment:
          type: number
        decision:
          type: string
        max_bid:
          type: number
        ml_probability:
          type: number
```

### 13.2 WebSocket Events

| Event | Direction | Payload |
|-------|-----------|---------|
| `pipeline:started` | Server â†’ Client | `{run_id, case_number}` |
| `pipeline:stage_complete` | Server â†’ Client | `{run_id, stage, result}` |
| `pipeline:complete` | Server â†’ Client | `{run_id, recommendation, max_bid}` |
| `pipeline:error` | Server â†’ Client | `{run_id, stage, error}` |

## 14. Technical Specifications

### 14.1 System Requirements

| Component | Minimum | Recommended |
|-----------|---------|-------------|
| Node.js | 18.x | 20.x |
| Python | 3.10 | 3.11+ |
| Memory | 2GB | 4GB |
| Storage | 10GB | 20GB |
| Network | 10 Mbps | 100 Mbps |

### 14.2 Dependencies

```
# Python Dependencies (requirements.txt)
langgraph>=0.2.0
langchain>=0.2.0
xgboost>=2.0.0
selenium>=4.15.0
httpx>=0.25.0
supabase>=2.0.0
python-docx>=1.0.0
pdfplumber>=0.10.0
curl_cffi>=0.7.0

# Node.js Dependencies (package.json)
next: 15.0.4
react: ^18.3.1
@anthropic-ai/sdk: ^0.32.0
@assistant-ui/react: ^0.7.0
@supabase/supabase-js: ^2.46.0
zustand: ^5.0.0
framer-motion: ^11.12.0
recharts: ^2.14.0
```

### 14.3 Configuration Reference

```yaml
# config/settings.yaml
biddeed:
  version: "2.0.0"
  environment: "production"
  
pipeline:
  max_concurrent: 5
  timeout_seconds: 300
  checkpoint_db: "checkpoints/biddeed.db"
  
smart_router:
  free_target: 0.45
  cheap_target: 0.35
  quality_target: 0.20
  default_tier: "FREE"
  
scrapers:
  beca:
    rate_limit: 10  # per minute
    retry_count: 3
    timeout: 30
  bcpao:
    rate_limit: 60
    cache_ttl: 604800  # 7 days
  acclaimweb:
    rate_limit: 5
    session_ttl: 1800
    
ml:
  model_version: "xgb_v1.0_64.4"
  confidence_threshold: 0.6
  feature_count: 28
  
database:
  url: "https://mocerqjnksmhcjzxrewo.supabase.co"
  pool_size: 10
  
monitoring:
  log_level: "INFO"
  metrics_enabled: true
  trace_sample_rate: 0.1
```

## 15. Appendices

### 15.1 Glossary

| Term | Definition |
|------|------------|
| ARV | After Repair Value - estimated property value after renovations |
| BECA | Brevard County E-Court Access system |
| BCPAO | Brevard County Property Appraiser's Office |
| Bid/Judgment Ratio | Max bid divided by final judgment amount |
| LangGraph | Framework for building stateful, multi-actor AI applications |
| Smart Router | Intelligent LLM tier selection system |
| The Everest Ascentâ„¢ | Proprietary 12-stage pipeline methodology |
| XGBoost | Gradient boosting ML algorithm |

### 15.2 Document History

| Version | Date | Author | Changes |
|---------|------|--------|---------|
| 1.0.0 | 2025-11-15 | AI Architect | Initial architecture |
| 1.5.0 | 2025-12-01 | AI Architect | Added Smart Router V5 |
| 2.0.0 | 2025-12-12 | AI Architect | Complete schema with C4 |
